msg:I took my family on a two-night and three-day trip to Wuzhen. The hotel I booked this time did not disappoint me and the experience was great. The hotel housekeeper will contact you on WeChat the day before departure and send you the navigation location and parking lot directions. After arriving at the parking lot, a hotel butler will be waiting to help guests carry their luggage and accompany them into the scenic spot. Because the hotel is located in the scenic area, the hotel will arrange to enter by boat, and there is a separate boat channel. There is no need to wait in line with other tourists, so you can quickly board the boatüö¢, board the boat and leave. It will take about ten minutes to reach the shore. Along the way You can also enjoy the scenery on both sides of the river on the boat. After the boat arrives, there will be another hotel steward waiting on the shore to help carry your luggage and bring it into the hotel. The boat stops directly in front of the hotel, which is very convenient. The whole process from the parking lot to the hotel takes about half an hour, which is worry-free and convenient. When leaving the hotel, you can also take a boat out of the scenic area at no charge.
The location of the hotel is excellent. It is in the center of Xizha Street, which is also the busiest place. It is very convenient to go out and visit the attractions. Although the outside of the hotel is very lively, the inside of the hotel is quiet and quiet, which will not affect your rest. We booked a superior double room. The view outside the window is very good. The lights will be turned on at night. The hotel's facilities are very complete and clean. The breakfast is an a la carte buffet, which means you will be given a menu to order. I think This kind is very good. You can order whatever you want without wasting it.
